- barrett_reduce_correct
-      : forall k : Z,
-        2 <= k ->
-        forall M muLow : Z,
-        0 < M ->
-        muLow + 2 ^ k = 2 ^ (2 * k) / M ->
-        0 <= muLow < 2 ^ k ->
-        2 ^ (k - 1) < M < 2 ^ k ->
-        2 * (2 ^ (2 * k) mod M) <= 2 ^ (k + 1) - (muLow + 2 ^ k) ->
-        forall n : nat,
-        n <> 0%nat ->
-        Z.of_nat n <= k ->
-        forall nout : nat,
-        nout = 2%nat ->
-        (forall i : nat, weight k 1 i = (2 ^ k) ^ Z.of_nat i) ->
-        forall xLow xHigh : Z,
-        0 <= xLow < 2 ^ k ->
-        0 <= xHigh < M ->
-        barrett_reduce k M muLow n nout xLow xHigh =
-        (xLow + 2 ^ k * xHigh) mod M
- Inductive ErrorMessage : Type :=
-     Computed_bounds_are_not_tight_enough : forall t : type,
-                                            partial.data t ->
-                                            partial.data t ->
-                                            forall s : type,
-                                            Expr (s -> t) ->
-                                            partial.data s ->
-                                            Pipeline.ErrorMessage
-   | Bounds_analysis_failed : Pipeline.ErrorMessage
-   | Type_too_complicated_for_cps : type -> Pipeline.ErrorMessage
-   | Value_not_le : string ->
-                    forall T' : Type, T' -> T' -> Pipeline.ErrorMessage
-   | Value_not_lt : string ->
-                    forall T' : Type, T' -> T' -> Pipeline.ErrorMessage
-   | Values_not_provably_distinct : string ->
-                                    forall T' : Type,
-                                    T' -> T' -> Pipeline.ErrorMessage
-   | Values_not_provably_equal : string ->
-                                 forall T' : Type,
-                                 T' -> T' -> Pipeline.ErrorMessage
- 
- For Computed_bounds_are_not_tight_enough: Arguments t, s are implicit and
-                                           maximally inserted
- For Value_not_le: Argument T' is implicit and maximally inserted
- For Value_not_lt: Argument T' is implicit and maximally inserted
- For Values_not_provably_distinct: Argument T' is implicit and maximally
-                                   inserted
- For Values_not_provably_equal: Argument T' is implicit and maximally inserted
- For Computed_bounds_are_not_tight_enough: Argument scopes are [ctype_scope _
-                                             _ ctype_scope Expr_scope _]
- For Type_too_complicated_for_cps: Argument scope is [ctype_scope]
- For Value_not_le: Argument scopes are [string_scope type_scope _ _]
- For Value_not_lt: Argument scopes are [string_scope type_scope _ _]
- For Values_not_provably_distinct: Argument scopes are [string_scope
-                                     type_scope _ _]
- For Values_not_provably_equal: Argument scopes are [string_scope type_scope _
-                                  _]
